Germany Indicates Readiness to Impose Economic Blockade; Albanian King Asks U.S. to Join Sanctions; League of Nations Forms Monitoring Committee

(Berlin) The government today issued a public statement that will please all countries, stating that Germany has blocked arms exports to Italy and Albania since the outbreak of the East African conflict and is now preparing to ban exports of raw materials and food at the appropriate time. It also stated that Germany's neutrality policy and attitude toward sanctions have not changed. It denied the statements made by the German consul in Geneva regarding the League of Nations' sanctions issue. (National Telegram, 7th)

(Geneva) A German spokesperson stated to the League of Nations Secretariat this afternoon that although the German government is not participating in the sanctions, it will attempt to prevent speculators from selling goods to Italy and Albania to make huge profits. This move means that Germany will indirectly cooperate with the League of Nations to implement economic sanctions against Italy. Representatives of various countries here were greatly pleased by Germany's first relaxation of its strict reservations. (National Telegram, 6th) The League of Nations announced today that Germany will find a way to prevent speculators from selling goods in the near future.

(Geneva) The German consul in Geneva notified the League of Nations that the German government has decided to comply with the measures passed by the Eighteen-Nation Committee regarding the transit of goods to Italy, which was announced by the Secretariat last night. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(New York) The Albanian King today sent a wireless message from the Albanian capital to the United States, requesting that the United States assist the League of Nations and join the sanctions, saying, "I do not ask others to draw swords against Italy, because the use of force is a method of ancient folly. The United States is not a member of the League of Nations, but it is time for the American public to assist the League of Nations in its efforts to seek peace, and there is also this opportunity. Our cause is humanitarian, and there is no dispute about it." (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull gave a radio address today, informing the nation and announcing that the United States remains outside the war, while using its appropriate influence to stop foreign wars. Hull explained the U.S. neutrality policy in the Italian-Ethiopian War and advocated that the president should have greater power to handle U.S. foreign policy during international disturbances. Some observers believe this argument to be a prelude to the authorities requesting the next Congress to pass a neutrality law that is broader in scope but more flexible than the current law. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

(Geneva) The Eighteen-Nation Committee formally approved the implementation of sanctions on November 18th today. The committee also formed a monitoring committee composed of representatives from the UK, France, Russia, Spain, Poland, Romania, Greece, Yugoslavia, and Sweden to monitor the implementation of sanctions and receive reports. Today's meeting removed newspapers, books, magazines, maps, musical scores, and other items from the list of prohibited imports from Italy. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Eighteen-Nation Committee Discusses Details of Sanctions, to Be Implemented Starting This Month on the 18th

(Geneva) The Eighteen-Nation Committee has passed the following four motions: (1) If non-member states agree to cooperate, the supply of oil, coal, steel, and iron will be stopped to Italy, and they will be added to the list of major commodities prohibited from being shipped to Italy. (2) Member states are required to make every effort to prevent prohibited goods from passing through their territories and being shipped to Italy. (3) A subcommittee will be formed to judge the requests made by member states to import Italian goods that have already been paid for. (4) It is recommended that member states temporarily suspend all current account agreements with Italy from November 18th to prevent Italy from purchasing goods abroad and obtaining new debts. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Geneva) Regarding (1) existing contracts with Italy, (2) the transit of goods to Italy, and (3) measures for offsetting debts with Italy, the Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee has yesterday passed the resolutions submitted by the various committees, stipulated the measures to be taken, and announced them to the public by the League of Nations Secretariat last night, as on file. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(Geneva) The Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee met this evening, chaired by Portuguese representative Vasco Gonçalves, and passed various measures regarding existing contracts with Italy, the transit of goods to Italy, and methods for offsetting debts with Italy. These measures were separately drafted by the various committees and were reported by Havas in the previous telegram. The Eighteen-Nation Committee then passed a proposal by the French representative stipulating that the ban on the import of Italian goods does not apply to books, newspapers, maps, and other printed materials. In addition, it was decided that the governments of each member state should submit reports on the various contracts signed with Italy by November 10th, and if there is a legitimate reason, the deadline may be extended to November 12th to submit a form listing the various contracts with Italy to the League of Nations for review and approval. (Havas dispatch, 6th)

(London) Foreign sources are rumored that the British-Iranian Oil Company (i.e., the Anglo-Persian Oil Company), the Dutch Oil Company, and the Mobil Oil Company are currently discussing the possibility of stopping the shipment of kerosene to Italy. However, people in the London oil industry do not believe this, saying that the United States cannot even control its domestic oil market. Therefore, Mobil Oil Company does not seem prepared to stop exports to Italy and allow small independent oil companies in California and Texas to rise up and replace them. Then their position would be enough to eliminate the effect of the oil embargo. Political observers consider the chance of banning kerosene shipments to Italy to be very slim. They believe that the United States will never do this. The only way is for the major oil companies to negotiate an agreement, but judging from the phenomenon, the companies seem to have no intention of doing so. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Thirty Miles North of Makale: Fierce Fighting Begins Between Italian and Abyssinian Armies; Abyssinian Army Resists Formally for the First Time; Italian Army Occupies All Surrounding Ridges

Addis Ababa: The Abyssinian authorities claim that the Abyssinian army is still holding Makale. The garrison is said to have withdrawn from the town during the day to avoid Italian air strikes and returned at night. (Reuters, 7th)

Asmara: The Italian army continued its advance along the entire northern front today and has captured the ridges controlling Makale. It has now occupied approximately 8,000 square miles of Abyssinian territory north of the Taigazi and Gobat rivers. These ridges are 9,000 feet above sea level. The Italian army plans to consolidate its gains from east to west tonight. (Reuters, 7th)

Addis Ababa: According to sources in the Abyssinian government today, there is guerrilla warfare northeast by north of Makale. Italian troops there have been driven back by troops under the command of Abyssinian Generals Seyoum and Gasa. (Reuters, 7th)

Italian Front Line, Northern Route: Yesterday, the vanguard of the Askaris advanced to the southwest of Haohe Town and charged with fixed bayonets. The Abyssinian army resisted bravely and did not retreat. Two white Italian officers were wounded, two Askari junior officers were killed, and ten Askari soldiers were injured. The number of Abyssinian casualties is unknown. This was the first formal resistance by the Abyssinian army. It is expected that the Abyssinian resistance will become increasingly fierce. The Italian army continued to attack successively at dawn today, but by 9:20 AM, there was no news from the front. (National Telegram, 7th)

Asmara: According to reports from Italian pilots, Makale appears to have been reoccupied by Abyssinian troops. After the Italian vanguard retreated from the town, the Abyssinian army re-entered and appears to be preparing to resist. Fierce fighting is taking place southwest of Hozien, approximately thirty miles north of Makale. Two Italian officers were wounded, two Italian colonial soldiers were killed, and ten were injured. Both sides engaged in fierce hand-to-hand combat with bayonets for a long time. The Abyssinian soldiers eventually fled, leaving many dead behind. This is the first time the Italian army has suffered casualties since adopting the new offensive. (Reuters, 7th)

(Rome): According to news received here today from Asmara, an Italian regiment arrived in Makale last night. (National Telegram, 6th)

Addis Ababa: The Abyssinian authorities expect the Italian army to launch a major offensive on both the northern and southern fronts. Although the current Italian advance is not very rapid, officials have acknowledged that the vanguard of the Italian army has reached the vicinity of the city of Makale. The city is about to be subjected to a large-scale attack. On the forward line in the Wogga Dan area, the weather has cleared, making military operations more convenient. The Abyssinian military preparations are actively underway, and a large number of foreign munitions will soon arrive. It is generally expected that in mid-November, the Italian and Abyssinian armies will have a major battle. The purpose is to seize several important strategic locations, or even to determine the outcome of the war in the middle of this month. (Havas, 6th)

Stalemate in Anglo-Italian Negotiations

Easing the Mediterranean Situation; Further Talks at an Appropriate Time

(London): The Cabinet today thoroughly considered the report from British Ambassador to Italy, Sir Eric Drummond, regarding his talks with Mussolini yesterday. It was decided that further discussions are needed before a concrete plan to end the tense situation between Britain and Italy can be determined. However, it is generally felt that some progress has been made towards establishing mutual goodwill. It is said that the tension between Britain and Italy and the situation in the Mediterranean are merely offshoots of the larger issue of ending the Italian-Abyssinian War. The talks between the British Ambassador to Italy and the Italian Prime Minister are still in the preliminary stages. Because both sides desire to achieve satisfactory progress, they will continue to meet when appropriate opportunities arise. (Reuters, 6th)

(Rome): Prime Minister Mussolini has held repeated talks with the British Ambassador to Italy, Sir Eric Drummond. According to responsible sources here, these talks have not resulted in any solution to the situation between Britain and Italy in the Mediterranean. (Havas, 7th)

(Paris): French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval today again attempted to mediate the Mediterranean crisis between Britain and Italy. Laval met separately with Italian Ambassador Cerruti and British Ambassador Clerk. It is reported that the Mediterranean issue was the most important topic discussed, but the content of the talks was not released. (National Telegram, 6th)

Predictions for the British General Election

(London): The general election campaign is now entering its final week. Judging by the current situation, the current government will still hold a majority of seats in Parliament. The Reuters parliamentary correspondent predicts the chances of the three major parties in the November 14th vote, stating his impressions as follows:

1. The Government party is confident of winning a majority. 2. The Labour party also admits that it would be very lucky to win. 3. The Liberal party is deeply concerned that the number of Liberal seats, already few, may continue to decline. The correspondent also stated that the reason for holding this election early is the result of the Abyssinian war. When Parliament adjourned for the summer recess in July, the government did not want to go to the people before next spring. At that time, the government had just been reorganized and deeply desired to wait a while to present concrete reasons regarding domestic policy to request the nation to grant it power. Several months ago, the current government was not absolutely secure. The opposition parties, taking advantage of the difficult unemployment situation and the government's calls to increase national defense forces, lobbied voters, which was quite unfavorable to the government. However, the Italian-Abyssinian conflict broke out, and the British government maintained peace and was regarded as the leader in Geneva. As a result, the most powerful tool used by the opposition parties to attack the government no longer existed. Because advocating for military preparations to defend peace, the government was supported by the opposition parties within a few weeks. As the election date approached, the position of the Labour and Liberal parties was not as good as before. All of their main tools used to attack the government were no more than the following five points: (1) The government is now taking advantage of the international situation to rush through its hoped-for winning election. (2) The government still has warmongering views and argues that the current situation shows that British military preparedness is insufficient, which is very dangerous, and will propose expanding military preparations if it regains power in the future. (3) The government is indecisive. If it had acted earlier in Geneva, the current crisis would not have occurred. (4) The government is implementing the Ottawa policy, which is economic imperialism, otherwise the current crisis would not have occurred. (5) The government's policy of relieving unemployment has failed. In normal times, this kind of tool used by the opposition parties would be enough to endanger the government's security. Industrial areas may favor the hardship of unemployment and disregard the Geneva peace talks during the election, and London has shown a tendency towards the Labour party in the recent city elections. However, international and domestic circumstances have made the government able to control the odds of winning. Supporters of the government believe that the government's policy of maintaining peace has received the support of the majority of organized labor, and the Liberal party also supports the government's measures in Geneva. Moreover, if the League of Nations fails, there will be all kinds of terrible possibilities for war. Therefore, the people must again grant the government great power before Christmas to help its prestige. Moreover, the government has promised (1) that if the League of Nations remains an effective organization, the United States will continue to support it; (2) to make the country fully prepared; (3) to propose new measures to relieve unemployment; (4) to provide special relief to disaster areas; (5) to improve social services. Furthermore, the government, which previously opposed raising the age of children leaving school, is now willing to reconsider it. All of these points should be understood by the people. (Reuters, 7th)

London Naval Conference to Open on December 5th; British Military Experts Begin Discussions; U.S. Secretary of the Navy Advocates Expanding Naval Forces

(London): Britain has proposed postponing the Naval Conference to December 5th. The conference will likely take a temporary break during Christmas and then reconvene early next year. The Italian representatives who arrived here yesterday have consulted with naval officials on naval limitation issues. It is understood that these discussions did not involve the current situation in the Mediterranean. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Washington): Secretary of the Navy Swanson stated today that he intends to maintain approximately 85% of the forces of all surface warships in peacetime, and the forces of submarines must be maintained in full. In the next budget, the Navy Department will recommend increasing the number of naval personnel to 100,000. As for whether the battleship Arkansas, which has exceeded its age, will be replaced by a new ship in 1937, this has not yet been decided. Swanson also stated that Secretary of War Dern, on his way back from the Philippines, will tour the key points of the Philippines, as well as Guam, Wake Island, Midway Island, and Honolulu, before returning to San Francisco in mid-December.

(Tokyo): The Ministry of Finance announced today that the expenses for Japan's participation in the London Naval Disarmament Conference will be 419,973 yuan. (Japan United Press, 7th)

(Geneva): League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol recently forwarded a note from British Foreign Secretary Hoare to all member states of the League of Nations and the countries attending the Disarmament Conference. The note stated: "The governments of the United States, Japan, France, and Italy, which signed the Washington and London Naval Treaties, have accepted the invitation of the British government to participate in the London Naval Conference, which will open on December 5th. The purpose of the conference is to limit the navies of various countries and revise the new treaty to replace the Washington and London Naval Treaties, which will expire at the end of 1936. The British government hopes that after the signatory countries of the Washington and London Naval Treaties have established a naval agreement, it will immediately invite representatives of other naval powers to participate in the conference." (Havas, 7th)

Shih Chao-chi's Speech: Promoting Sino-American Friendship

Boston: Chinese Ambassador to the United States Shih Chao-chi delivered a speech to the China Society here today, stating that American goodwill towards China has promoted American trade with China since 1931 and has achieved the leading position of Britain and Japan, accounting for more than 22% of China's foreign trade. It increased to 26% in 1934, at which time Japan accounted for only 12.5% and Britain accounted for 12%. Americans have never taken advantage of China's crisis to seek selfish gains. We are very satisfied. American businessmen and manufacturers deeply know that goodwill is the key to trade. Americans spend huge sums of money annually to establish schools and hospitals in China, creating psychological factors of goodwill. This is purely out of charitable motives. However, it is also a fact that Chinese goodwill towards America promotes Sino-American trade. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Rome): According to news received by various newspapers here from Asmara, East Africa, it has been confirmed that the Abyssinian garrison of Makale has begun to withdraw. Italian aircraft flying over the city have discovered a white flag hanging in the central square, indicating surrender. At present, two vanguard teams of the Italian army have arrived under the city of Makale, but it is not expected that they will occupy it until tomorrow morning. After the Italian army captures Makale, it will continue to advance south to Lake Ashangi, 100 kilometers away, to place the entire province of Tigray under Italian control. A large force is currently advancing towards Makale, but is proceeding cautiously, fearing ambush by Abyssinian troops. (Havas, 7th)

International Financial Circles Pay Attention to the Dynamics of the Chinese Exchange Market

No Change in British Policy towards China; Denies Establishment of Loan Between China and Britain

(London): International financial experts today are paying close attention to the dynamics of the foreign exchange markets in Shanghai and Hong Kong to judge whether China's nationalization of silver and currency management policies can succeed. In general, China's currency is currently quite stable, but it is generally believed here that this is due to British support. As for the real results, they cannot be seen until after a long period of time. However, since British merchant banks can assist, China's exchange rate with Britain and the United States should be able to maintain a stable price for a considerable period of time. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Tokyo): According to semi-official Japanese sources, British Ambassador to Japan Clive, when meeting with the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs today, firmly denied the claim that Britain had loaned China 10 million pounds. He also said that Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, a British economic expert currently in China, has nothing to do with China's decision to nationalize silver. As far as the Chinese incident is concerned, Britain is willing to continue to exchange opinions with Japan on China's financial and political situation. In short, Britain does not want to have any history of changing its policy toward China. (Reuters, 6th)

(Tokyo): Regarding China's currency reform, the meeting between Ambassador Arima and Minister Kong Xiangxi, as well as the talks between the British Ambassador to Japan and Vice Minister Shigemitsu, have clarified that there is no agreement between China and Britain to establish a loan or set up credit. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now understood the true intention of Britain. (Dentsu, 7th)

(London): Today's Times editorial stated that the Chinese government's financial and monetary reforms should receive the unanimous support of all countries that care about China's welfare. Unfortunately, the first reports transmitted to Tokyo immediately caused misunderstandings. In any case, it has been partially dispelled by the declaration that no British loan has been made and that Japan's rights have not been ignored. Japan must know that if China can reorganize its currency system through its own efforts, Japan can also benefit, no different from others. There are still many thorns in the road ahead, and China still needs all the support it can get to implement this reform. (Reuters, 7th)

(Washington): A Washington Daily News political reporter, after inspecting silver-producing states, announced today that the U.S. silver purchase plan is disappointing everywhere. Comparing China's monetary contraction with the benefits promoted by those who support the government's silver policy, he said that even silver merchants across the country do not like this policy. (National Telegram, 6th)

Behind-the-Scenes Controversy Over U.S. Silver Purchase Policy

(Washington): It was heard today from well-informed sources that amid an atmosphere in which some people have doubts about China's ability to implement the national silver policy, the U.S. Treasury Department is now watching foreign developments and does not want to draw any conclusions about the final outcome arising from the U.S. silver policy. Although the U.S. government is closely watching the situation, it is not issuing criticisms. It appears that the question of whether the U.S. has driven China to adopt this policy has aroused behind-the-scenes controversy. Those who defend the U.S. government say that China's troubles are its internal affairs, while those who criticize the government say that the U.S. silver policy is responsible for China's steps. As of now, the U.S. government has not received any documents from American banks and other businessmen in China requesting assistance to protect their silver holdings. (Reuters, 6th)

(New York): The Bank Daily published a long article today ridiculing the government's silver policy, saying that the government's silver policy has not only failed to restore the monetary prestige of silver, but has harmed it. China's national silver policy is a response to this policy, and its impact has shattered illusions. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Washington): A Washington Daily News political reporter, after inspecting silver-producing states, announced today that the U.S. silver purchase plan is disappointing everywhere. Gold and Silver

English Gold: The London gold price today was 141 shillings, 5 and a half pence, up one penny.

English Silver: The London silver market was stable today. The spot price was unchanged at 29 and 3125 pence. Futures rose by 1875 to 29 and 125 pence. US purchases and speculative trading were both active, and supply was not abundant.

Exchange Rates

US-UK: The London foreign exchange market was very quiet this morning. The exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar opened at $4.918125, up 1875. At 2 pm, this price remained unchanged.

UK-France: The opening was unchanged at 74 francs 65. It fell two pounds pu after one hour, and no further changes were seen at 2 pm.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened higher, rising seven points due to good Alexandria telegrams. It continued to rise due to poor weather reports. The force of short selling was not strong, and the previous gains were maintained. New York Cotton Exchange brokers estimate the total cotton production for this season to be 11.30.

English Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market also rose slightly. In the afternoon, the January futures were 6.14, up two points.

English Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was stable today. At 1 pm, December futures rose half a penny to 6 shillings and 1 and 625 pence.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened sharply higher. The first lot price was 625 higher than yesterday's close, but fell by half a point due to increased short selling. Coarse grains also opened higher by two and a half points, but then showed signs of fatigue like the wheat market.

Rubber

London: London rubber opened stable this morning. The trading price for January-March futures was 6 and 9375 pence, up 0625 from yesterday's close. No change at noon.

New York: The New York rubber market opened eight points higher this morning, and the market was quite stable. The London price was firm, so there were many orders to fill positions here, leading to a further rise of four points. After the bulls slightly closed their positions, the price fell back by two points.

Securities

New York: The New York stock market opened sharply higher this morning, especially entertainment stocks. Loew's Cinema stocks rose 2.25 immediately after opening because the company announced that it would issue a special dividend of 50 cents per share. Morning trading was not as active as in the past few days, and there was profit-taking, so various securities plummeted later. Scientific Musings

—Edited by Li Yinkong and Ma Dapu of the Science Society of China

Forests and Human Life

On land, areas where trees that produce timber grow densely are called forests. The trees are called forest trees, and the land is called forest land. Therefore, a forest is actually the general term for forest trees and forest land.

In ancient times, the population was sparse, and almost the entire vast land was covered by forests. Therefore, forest products, both primary and secondary, could be taken without end and used inexhaustibly. This was the golden age of forests. Later, as the population increased, forest products gradually became insufficient to meet demand. As a result, nomadic herding and farming gradually developed. Forest land was reclaimed, and forest trees were consumed. This was the initial decline of forests. Furthermore, forests gradually decreased due to the development of agriculture, and humans, misunderstanding forests as useless objects that hindered reclamation, wantonly cut down and burned them, making it increasingly difficult to obtain timber. This was the gradual decline of forests. By the time people became wiser, and industry and commerce developed, the need for timber increased daily, and its uses became more widespread. Merchants then engaged in large-scale logging, leading to forest devastation, exposed mountains, and consequent impacts such as river blockage, mountain collapse, and climate imbalance, making people feel not only the timber shortage.

Forests were destroyed due to the increase in human population, as briefly described above. However, as human life depends on forests and the harm of forest depletion became apparent, the science of forest construction began to emerge. The relationship between forests and humans is divided into two categories, direct and indirect, as described below.

(1) Direct Relationship between Forests and Human Life

Producing timber is the main product of forests and an indispensable item in human life. Whether it is construction timber, transportation materials, or anything needed for our daily necessities, few can be made without timber. In recent years, with scientific progress, the use of timber has gradually expanded, such as decomposing timber into wood pulp for papermaking, weaving, and manufacturing rayon and artificial ivory, or dry-distilling timber to extract tar, wood vinegar, wood spirit, and acetone as industrial raw materials. Recently, timber has even been used as a raw material for making sugar and brewing wine. Therefore, the use of timber is expanding daily and is extremely important and significant to our clothing, food, housing, and transportation.

Providing Byproducts: In addition to timber as its main product, forests can also produce byproducts, such as paper made from mulberry bark, oil extracted from paulownia seeds, edible toon leaves, and rosin made from pine resin. Other valuable foods and medicines such as shiitake mushrooms, silver ear fungus, cinnamon, and magnolia bark are also products of trees. The birds and animals that inhabit the forest, and the edible fungi and undergrowth that grow on the forest floor, are also important byproducts of the forest.

Developing Capital and Accommodating Labor: Forests are a type of large enterprise and an important part of the national economy. Their capital includes forest trees and the forest land where they grow. Any land unsuitable for crop growth can be afforested. It is estimated that the world's forest area is about 7.5 billion acres. With such a vast area of forest land, the large amount of capital required each year for afforestation, harvesting, logging, and other work, and the manufacturing of its byproducts, and the large number of workers accommodated, can be imagined. It is reported that the United States recruited 300,000 unemployed unmarried young people in 1933 to engage in forestry work. The budget for that year was 250 million yuan. In addition, the central government's regular forestry budget was as much as US$36,325,323.

(2) Indirect Relationship between Forests and Human Life

Harmonizing Climate: According to experiments by experts from Europe and the United States, the temperature in forests is usually cooler during the day and warmer at night, cooler in summer and warmer in winter, compared to outside the forest. Because the forest floor is covered by tree crowns, sunlight cannot directly shine on the forest floor, so the heat of the sun is not easily penetrated. At night, the heat inside the forest is also difficult to dissipate due to the coverage of branches and leaves. Therefore, due to the gradual flow of air, the temperature inside the forest is harmonized, and the temperature near the forest is also affected, forming a mild forest climate. As for humidity, because forests can store a large amount of water, they are also higher than non-forested areas, which can increase the amount of rainfall in the area and reduce the harm of prolonged drought and prolonged rain. This is how forests harmonize the climate.

Conserving Water Sources: Because forests have lush trees, when it rains, rainwater first falls on the tree crowns and then slowly drips into the forest. As a result of the delayed flow of rainwater, in addition to the ground cover being able to absorb as much water as possible, a large amount of water can also penetrate into the ground, be absorbed and stored by the roots of trees, and slowly flow out. Therefore, even in prolonged droughts, there are constant springs near forests.

Protecting Soil: Because the roots of forest trees spread and extend, they can strengthen the binding force of the soil, so even the soil on sloping hillsides will not collapse due to rain. Moreover, the tree crowns of forests and the ground cover in the forest cover the ground, preventing it from being directly hit by rainwater. The rainfall slowly enters the forest through the tree crowns. In addition to being absorbed by the forest cover and penetrating into the soil, the amount of rainwater flowing out is small and slow, and there is no force to erode the soil. Therefore, there is no risk of denudation where there are forests.

Reducing Flood and Drought Disasters: The reasons for the formation of floods are nothing more than a sudden increase in water volume and river channel siltation. Since forests can conserve water sources, part of the rainfall is absorbed by the forest during heavy rain and prolonged rain, so the amount of water in rivers will not increase suddenly. Moreover, since forests can protect the soil, the water flowing out of the forest will not carry sand and soil to fill the riverbed. As for the causes of drought disasters, they are nothing more than a lack of rainfall and a lack of groundwater. Forests can increase the amount of rainfall and store a large amount of groundwater, which gradually flows into streams. Therefore, forests have considerable effectiveness in preventing floods and droughts.

Preventing Wind and Sand and Avalanches: On vast coasts or plains, if there are no forests to provide shelter, sand and soil will fly around during storms, harming people and property, which is very dangerous. If forests are lush, the expansion of tree branches and leaves will inevitably reduce the ability of wind and sand to move. If forests can be built on sandy land, the mechanical action of tree roots to settle soil and sand is the best strategy. For example, the Gascony region of France has 800,000 acres of land that is entirely a sandy area. Since 1810, this wind and sand prevention forest has been built and has now become the first forest area in France. Also, in cold mountainous areas, snow accumulates in winter and does not melt. When the weather warms in spring, the snow melts and moves down the mountain, damaging people's lives and property. If there are trees to provide shelter, the snow on the mountain will be supported by the trees and will not fall and cause avalanches.

Enhancing Scenery: Forests are an element that makes up scenery and have a unique aesthetic, so they can cultivate our temperament. Moreover, because the forest scene is solemn and quiet, the residents near the forest are also influenced by it and are rich in a spirit of courage and simplicity. Therefore, the ancients said that beautiful mountains and rivers produce great people, and also said that the heart is at ease in the mountains, which is the meaning of this.

Benefiting Hygiene: Air is an indispensable element in our lives, so whether the air is clean or not has a great impact on human life. Trees can separate oxygen through photosynthesis to meet human needs, and the forest contains a large amount of ozone, which can eliminate unclean gases, smoke, and harmful bacteria. Therefore, it is no coincidence that people living in the mountains are often healthy and long-lived.

Protecting Fishing and Hunting: Forests are the place where wild birds and animals live and feed. Without forests, birds and animals would have no place to rely on. Therefore, the relationship between forests and birds and animals is easily recognized by us. As for the relationship between forests and fish, the fruits and leaves that fall from the forest flow into rivers with the water, which is sufficient for fish to eat. The shadows of the forest cast on the water surface can be used for fish to rest. Moreover, forests can regulate the amount of water in rivers to prevent riverbeds from being buried, and can also promote the growth and reproduction of aquatic mosses, aquatic plants, and microorganisms, such as the genus Aponogeton distachyos, to provide food for fish. They can also regulate the temperature of rivers and prevent river water from carrying sand and mud, which is of no small benefit to fish health.

Improving Soil: Forests can transform low-lying and dry land into suitable production land. For example, in marshy areas, only the water needs to be drained once, and then suitable tree species can be planted to create a wetland forest. The evaporation of the tree crowns can make the moisture in the soil suitable. As for loose, dry, and barren sandy land, drought-resistant tree species or legumes can also be planted. The soil can also be improved by the action of fallen leaves, dead branches, and root nodules of legumes fixing nitrogen in the forest. For example, the coast of East Prussia in Germany was once a barren sandy area. After the government vigorously implemented afforestation, it has now become a source of productive benefits. The effectiveness of forest soil improvement can be seen from this.

Facilitating Navigation: With the development of modern navigation, lighthouses and buoys are installed in important harbors, islands, and capes to ensure the safety of waterways. However, in places without these targets, the shape of the land is often used as a standard. Forests are higher than the land and are actually the best navigation targets.

The importance of forests to human life has been described above. According to the Ministry of Industry, the area of wasteland suitable for forestry in our country is no less than 500 million mu, accounting for almost one-third of the total area of the country. How should we work hard to engage in afforestation and protect wild trees in this large area of wasteland to increase production, directly prevent our clothing, food, housing, and transportation from lacking raw materials, and indirectly ensure our safety in life?

The Situation in Wuhan After the Implementation of Legal Tender

Commodity Prices Rise, Copper Coins Scarce; Authorities Order Strict Crackdown

Hankou Communication: Since the 4th, upon receiving the order from the Ministry of Finance to implement legal tender, the market in Wuhan has been relatively stable. Various commercial banks, such as the Yanye (Salt Industry), Siming, Dalu (Continental), Nonggong (Agriculture and Industry), Guohuo (National Products), Nongshang (Agriculture and Commerce), Shangye (Commerce), Meifeng, Jin Cheng (Gold City), Shanghai, Shiye (Industry), Zhongnan (Central South), Tongshang (Trade), Nongmin (Farmer), Dafu, Dazhong (Great Central), Bianye (Border Industry), Juxingcheng, Zhejiang Xingye (Zhejiang Development), and Zhejiang Shiye (Zhejiang Industry) banks, as well as the Hubei Provincial Bank, have all complied with the order to submit detailed reports of their cash reserves and the amount of banknotes issued up to November 3rd. Foreign banks, such as Citibank of the United States and HSBC of the United Kingdom, are also accepting and disbursing legal tender. It is reported that the total silver reserves in the city are approximately 20 million yuan. The Central, China, and Communications Banks, in addition to accepting cash at their branches, are uniformly exchanging the silver reserves of various commercial banks for legal tender, which is expected to be completed within about a week. Today, the Central Bank headquarters transported several million yuan of legal tender to assist various banks in meeting withdrawals. The Bankers Association held an emergency meeting today and decided on six points: (1) Each bank shall prepare three separate tables listing in detail their cash, savings, and issuance reserves as of November 3rd, and submit them to the Bankers Association for forwarding to the Municipal Government and the Central Bank. The types of banknotes shall be classified as "Shen" banknotes, "Han" banknotes, and subsidiary currency notes, and the cash shall be classified as raw silver, silver dollars, and copper coins. If there are items held in trust for others, they shall be reported separately in accordance with the above procedures and submitted to the Association within seven days; (2) Hereafter, all bills and contracts issued by banks shall be written with the words "National Currency." Bills and contracts issued previously, as well as bills and contracts issued by customers hereafter, which still use words such as "Ocean Silver," "Silver Dollar," "Shen Banknote," and "Han Banknote," shall be regarded as National Currency and accepted using banknotes from the Central, China, and Communications Banks and banknotes approved by the Ministry of Finance for continued circulation by banks other than the three banks; (3) Once the inventory of each bank has been reported, if there is any exchange for legal tender thereafter, the inventory amount must be changed. The three banks shall prepare a two-part exchange certificate, with one part kept as a stub and the other given to the exchanger as proof. Before the exchange certificate is printed, a temporary slip shall be used as proof. For exchanges made in the previous two days, a receipt shall be issued retroactively; (4) Interbank accounts shall be consolidated into National Currency accounts, and interest shall be calculated up to the date of consolidation; (5) Due to the scarcity of copper coins in the market, the government is requested to prohibit imports and exports and stipulate the legal exchange rate; (6) The three banks should not limit the remittance of banknotes only to their own branches. The three banks shall accept all remittances using banknotes from the three banks and banknotes approved by the Ministry of Finance for continued circulation by banks other than the three banks. As for the Reserve Fund Custody Committee, there is no need for it in Wuhan at present, and the banking sector has not made any requests. The three banks have not yet considered handling real estate mortgages and will decide based on future developments. During this period of sudden implementation of legal tender, the Wuhan market is extremely panicked by two things: one is the rise in commodity prices, and the other is the lack of copper coins. The prices of various commodities are rising, especially the prices of food such as rice and flour, which are rising sharply, causing losses to the common people. The lack of copper coins is particularly difficult, and disputes arise from time to time in retail trade. Today, government officials and merchants held a special joint emergency meeting to discuss relief measures. Mayor Wu Guozhen, Chamber of Commerce Chairman Huang Wenzhi, committee members Zhou Xingtang, Chen Jinghui, Zhu Yongzhai, Cao Yanxiang, Zhu Futian, Deng Xizhou, Bankers Association Chairman Wang Xipu Xinya, and Money Dealers Association Chairman Wang Xinfuli attended. It was resolved to prohibit the outflow of copper coins from the Wuhan urban area, and violators will be investigated and punished, and the copper coins will be confiscated. The legal price of copper coins will be permanently fixed at 6 strings of cash per National Currency yuan, and violators will be prosecuted for disrupting the financial order. Those who deliberately hoard large amounts and manipulate the market will be severely punished, and if necessary, 100-wen subsidiary currency will be printed for circulation. As for the increase in commodity prices, strict measures will also be taken. After the meeting, the Municipal Government issued a proclamation stating: "Regarding the matter of this currency reform and the centralization of reserves, we have forwarded the telegrams from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and the Ministry of Finance, and announced them to the public. Since the implementation in recent days, market transactions have been as usual, indicating that people from all walks of life thoroughly understand that this policy is a necessary measure to improve finance, save the nation, and preserve its existence. However, there are occasional cases of a few citizens raising commodity prices and hoarding copper coins, thinking that the centralization of cash is still the same as in 1926 and 1927. It must be known that the measures determined this time are completely different from those in 1926 and 1927. In 1926 and 1927, the centralization of cash in Wuhan was only limited to Wuhan, and cash was still used elsewhere. Even in Wuhan, foreigners refused to accept banknotes, so banknotes and cash formed two kinds of market prices, the paper currency depreciated, and commodity prices rose. Now that legal tender is implemented, the whole country is unified, and all foreign banks also comply with it, and the customs duties are standardized. People holding legal tender can exchange goods everywhere. In the past, the currency system was not unified, and those who remitted funds to various places had to pay a surcharge, but now they can all be used. Therefore, after the implementation of legal tender, commodity prices not only cannot rise but are also more balanced than before. In recent years, the domestic economy has been affected by silver externally and by major droughts and floods internally. The purchasing power of the people is weak, and the market is becoming increasingly sluggish. The increase in commodity prices depends on the existence of economic strength. With weak purchasing power, even if commodity prices are raised, there will be no market and losses will inevitably be incurred. At present, due to the initial misunderstanding of the legal tender policy, there is a rush to hoard goods, and commodity prices have risen as a result. It is important to know that this is only a temporary phenomenon. If hoarding continues, the market will be stable as usual, and commodity prices will eventually fall. Who will bear this loss? As for copper coins, they are a kind of subsidiary currency. If the price of legal tender is stable, how can subsidiary currency be raised independently? Knowing that hoarding is a foolish idea. As the mayor serving my hometown, it is my duty to send personnel to secretly investigate unscrupulous merchants who raise commodity prices and hoard copper coins, and severely punish them according to law at any time. It is necessary to issue a sincere proclamation to inform the public." Moreover, the Pacification Commissioner's Office ordered the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters and the Hankou Municipal Government to immediately consult with responsible personnel from the Chamber of Commerce to properly plan measures to restore the original state, stating: "After the implementation of the new currency policy, the economic situation in various places has been very stable. However, in Wuhan, a few merchants are taking the opportunity to profit, manipulating copper coins, purchasing goods with small banknotes, refusing to give change, and privately setting up dark markets to raise commodity prices. If this continues, the market and finance will stagnate, and the people's livelihood will become more difficult. The state's currency reform was originally intended to save the crisis and revive the economy, but the general public has not fully understood the truth, resulting in unscrupulous elements taking the opportunity to hoard goods. If this is not stopped immediately, it will undermine the currency system and affect public security. Considering the future, it is very dangerous. The said commander and mayor are instructed to immediately consult with responsible personnel from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce to properly plan measures and quickly restore the original state. If it is found that there is hoarding of copper coins, seeking to profit, and raising commodity prices while depreciating legal tender, they will be treated as crimes against the Republic of China. This matter concerns public security and is not trivial. It is ordered that the said commander and mayor handle it together and report back as necessary." (6th)

Large Numbers of Refugees from Shandong Province Pass Through

On the morning of the 7th, over two hundred refugees, men, women, old, and young, from Yilin County, Shandong Province, arrived near the Wuxi-Shanghai Motor Company, looking wretched. On the morning of the 6th, he took his own car from Zhenjiang along the Zhen-Cheng Road to Dangyang, where Wu Tingzu, the Tianwu Road project director, welcomed him at the train station. In the afternoon, he returned to Zhenjiang in the same car. Hangzhou

Standardizing Ocean Prices to Stabilize Finance

The Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce, seeing that the local finance was quite chaotic after the Ministry of Finance implemented the currency reform and that unscrupulous merchants were taking the opportunity to raise commodity prices, convened a joint meeting of various industries on the evening of the 6th and decided: (1) Each legal tender will be exchanged for 12 jiao of small ocean silver, each small ocean silver will be exchanged for 25 copper coins, and each legal tender will be exchanged for 300 copper coins; (2) To take care of the livelihood of exchange shops, a handling fee of 1 fen will be charged for each legal tender exchanged in the retail market, whether entering or leaving, to be paid by the exchanger; (3) All transactions shall be based on the standard price of legal tender, and no increase or decrease shall be allowed; (4) Starting from the 7th, all trade associations will be notified to implement this uniformly. The Central, China, and Communications Banks also convened a joint meeting of the banking and money industries on the 7th and decided: (1) Starting today, all banks and firms in the city will set up places to exchange cash for banknotes to facilitate citizens; (2) The issue of insufficient currency in various industries will be addressed by the banking and money industries associations sending a letter to the three banks to forward to the head office for review and then holding a meeting to discuss relief methods.

Jiaxing

County Government Meeting to Collect Hard Currency

Since the Ministry of Finance announced the implementation of currency reform in Jiaxing, the prices of goods in the market have suddenly risen, and people's hearts are unsettled. Hard currency is still used as usual in market transactions. County Magistrate Wang Xianqiang specially convened a meeting on the 7th with Qian Boying, the manager of the local Bank of China, Wang Jingxiu, the manager of the local bank, Shen Xianheng, the manager of the Farmers Bank, Jiang Fuqing, the representative of the County Chamber of Commerce, and others to discuss methods for collecting hard currency. It was decided: (1) The deadline for all kinds of hard currency is the end of November, and the use of hard currency in the market will be stopped; (2) The Bank of China, the local bank, and the Farmers Bank will be responsible for the collection; (3) The branch offices of the Farmers Bank in Wangjiangjing, Xincheng, Xinfeng, and Wangdian will collect on behalf of the banks; (4) The public security organs will collect on behalf of the banks in remote rural areas.

Educational Broadcasting Special Issue

— Inscribed by Wang Shijie

Youth and the Nation (Part 2)

(Lecture to secondary school students nationwide on October 29th and 31st)

Qian Duansheng, Professor at Central University

The third flaw of our nation is the pervasiveness of callousness. Callousness is related to selfishness. We Chinese people have an idiom that says "Mingzhe baoshen" (wise men protect themselves), and a couplet that says "Each sweeps the snow from his own doorstep, and cares not for the frost on his neighbor's roof." These can both describe the spirit with which a class of people conducts themselves in their dealings with others. I remember a few years ago, a Mr. Weng was traveling by car from Nanjing to Hangzhou when the car overturned, and Mr. Weng was seriously injured. After several tens of minutes, a car sped by, completely ignoring Mr. Weng, who was groaning and begging for help. This kind of callousness is extremely common in China. However, this shortcoming is enough to make our nation one that lacks initiative, courage, and unity.

Speaking of our country's land, it has both good and bad aspects. The good aspect is that our country has a vast area, and we have lands in the cold, temperate, and hot zones. But we must also be aware of our shortcomings. We often boast that our land is vast and abundant, but in reality, while our land is large, our resources are not abundant. Although we, the Soviet Union, and the United States are all large countries, in terms of surface products and underground deposits, our country cannot compare with the United States and the Soviet Union. Underground coal, iron, and oil, as well as above-ground forests, are all essential elements for modern wealthy and powerful countries, but our country's supply is not abundant. Even in terms of agricultural products, our country's output is lower than that of the two countries, and the United States does not often have floods or droughts, the Soviet Union rarely has floods or droughts, while floods and droughts are common occurrences in our country. The Yellow River's floods have persisted for thousands of years, and there has been no solution. The Yangtze River's floods were not common in the past, but in recent years, due to the siltation of the major lakes and the encroachment of local bullies and gentry on lakeside fields, the river water often overflows. Therefore, we must not be proud of our vast land and abundant resources. Our land is large, but our productivity is not. To enhance our country's position, we must work hard to prevent floods, promote afforestation, increase agricultural productivity, and invent substitutes for petroleum.

Speaking of sovereignty, we should be familiar with the history of how sovereignty has been violated in recent decades, as well as the process of losing sovereignty. As I just mentioned, sovereignty is one of the elements of an independent country. But in recent decades, foreign consular officials or judicial officials have enjoyed jurisdiction over trials on Chinese territory. Foreigners who commit crimes in China are not tried in Chinese courts, but in foreign offices. Foreigners also have the right to station troops in China. More recently, foreigners can undermine the integrity of our territory and the unity of administrative power; and can insist that we do something, or not allow us to do something else. This kind of infringement on sovereignty is enough to deprive our country of its independence and turn it into a semi-independent country.

Knowing the state of our people, land, and sovereignty is essential to understanding our country's loveliness, and also its worries. Our country has a large population, a great nation, and a vast area. This kind of country is worthy of our love, and we can be proud of it. But our nation has shortcomings, the land's resources are not abundant, and our sovereignty is not complete; these are truly worthy of our concern. Young people—your first task to the nation is to love and save the country, and you must strive to be familiar with everything about the nation. Only by understanding China can you love China; only by understanding China can you save China!

(II) Be a Good Citizen

The deeper the understanding of the country, the stronger the patriotism will naturally be. However, merely having strong patriotism is not enough to shoulder the great responsibility of saving the country. Young people must work harder to be good citizens, and strive to attain the cultivation of a citizen. As mentioned above, our nation has many major shortcomings. If the Chinese people are to progress and become better citizens, the young people who will be the future masters of the country should naturally aspire to be model citizens.

There are many conditions for being a good Chinese citizen, and a model citizen of the future. The following six are especially important:

First, young people should have a spirit of cooperation. The spirit of cooperation is what was formerly called the spirit of collectivity. The Chinese have always lacked this spirit. The inability of the Chinese to cooperate is evident everywhere. In the political sphere, political parties are not easy to develop in China, because the Chinese have always been "friends but not partisans." Political associations of a few people are easy to have, but common political life of many people is difficult. In the commercial sphere, sound company systems are also not easy to develop. It's not that the Chinese are incapable of doing business, but that they simply cannot cooperate in doing business. The reasons why the Chinese lack a spirit of cooperation are not simple. The lack of development of education is an important reason, but the biggest reasons are two: one is the lack of training in cooperation, and the other is the lack of a habit of obeying rules and believing in rules. Therefore, to cultivate a spirit of cooperation, one must have training in cooperation in youth, and must absolutely obey the rules.

Today's youth are receiving education in schools, and schools are the best place to train in cooperation. In schools, there are various meetings and various groups. The purpose of establishing these meetings and groups may be very simple and ordinary, but young people should not despise them. They should fully participate in activities, because in these seemingly purposeless meetings or groups, young people can most easily gain experience in collective life and training in cooperation. This experience and this training are the foundation of all future cooperation.

The spirit of adhering to rules is also a fundamental condition for cooperation among people. Without the spirit of adhering to rules, cooperation cannot have sustainability or a larger scale. The unity of a few people can still be maintained by emotion, but the union of many people must have rules that are commonly observed. To use political parties and companies as metaphors, for a political party to maintain its party organization and promote its platform, it relies entirely on its platform. The ability of party members to obey the party's rules is party discipline. If party members do not abide by party discipline, the party organization will inevitably be divided and the party's platform will be impossible to promote. For a company to maintain its position, shareholders must also absolutely abide by the company's articles of association. If shareholders refuse to follow certain articles of association and always plan for themselves, the company will inevitably decline or go bankrupt. If the prosperity of political parties and companies requires a spirit of adhering to rules, then all other group life even more requires this spirit. If the rules are prescribed in this way, we should do it in this way, even if it is unfavorable to ourselves, we should have a spirit of sacrifice; even if it hinders friendship and personal relations, we can only not show it. The Chinese people have always valued personal feelings most, which is fundamentally in conflict with the spirit of complying with laws and regulations. Young people should be warned in the county, otherwise the spirit of cooperation cannot be developed or cultivated.

Second, young people should have a martial spirit. Our Chinese nation is inherently peace-loving, and peace is also an excellent national characteristic. We should of course preserve it. Moreover, we want a world of universal harmony, and all the world's nations should advocate peace, but the world today is not a peaceful world, and our China is an oppressed country. These are all facts. The Premier strongly advocated universal harmony and pacifism, but he also argued that we should first strive for national equality. The reason why he has this view is because the Chinese nation, if it cannot achieve equality, can never stand up for the oppressed nations of the world. He said: "We oppressed nations must restore our nation's free and equal status before we are qualified to talk about cosmopolitanism." Cosmopolitanism here means universal harmony. I dare say: if we do not know martial arts and cannot defend ourselves, then there will absolutely be no place for our country in this world, let alone universal harmony.

The advocacy of a martial spirit in our country also has a history of thirty or forty years. Since China was defeated by Japan in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894, a group of enlightened people have advocated martial arts. After Japan defeated Russia in the Russo-Japanese War, people who had received a new education even more strongly advocated this spirit. Gymnastics as a subject became popular at this time, and schools were required to set up gymnastics classes. However, despite the long history of promoting a martial spirit, in reality our nation still lacks a martial spirit. What is the reason for this? This is because, on the one hand, the traditional disdain of Chinese scholars for soldiers is too deeply rooted, and on the other hand, the military in these decades has really made people look down on them. Now that the country's life is in extreme danger, and the reputation of the military is far better than before, young people who are studying should correct the past mistakes of scholars. Scholars should regard being a soldier as the most honorable thing. The so-called martial spirit does not mean participating in sports and training the body. Doing more sports and training a strong body is certainly very important, but young people today should prepare to be soldiers, prepare to defend the country with their weapons; otherwise, they cannot be good citizens. This is the true meaning of a martial spirit.

Third, young people should have a spirit of enjoying labor. The so-called scholar-officials of China in the past, the scholars of China in the past, not only looked down on being soldiers, but also looked down on working. People with knowledge are unwilling to be soldiers, which is enough to lead to the demise of the country. People with knowledge look down on labor, which can also lead to the demise of the country. We must know that China is a country with backward industry and agriculture. The backwardness of industry and agriculture is no less than the backwardness of military equipment in leading to the demise of the country, or even more than the backwardness of military equipment. Because countries with developed industry and agriculture can easily replenish their military equipment, as long as the people have a martial spirit. If industry and agriculture are not developed, even if the people have a martial spirit, it is not easy to have good military equipment. We can cite a few examples. The United States is a country with extremely developed industry and agriculture that does not have a standing army, but after the United States declared war on Germany in 1917, it trained more than three million excellent troops within a year. The Abyssinians are a very martial and warlike people, but because their industry and agriculture are extremely underdeveloped, Italy dares to bully them. I dare say that if Abyssinia's industry and agriculture had half the level of Italy's industry and agriculture, Italy would not dare to bully them. Our country is also a country with backward industry and agriculture. This is also the main reason why our country is bullied.

Therefore, with only a military and without the backing of industry and agriculture, the freedom and equality of the nation can never be obtained. But to develop industry and agriculture, it is not enough to rely on people without knowledge to work hard as workers and farmers. There must be people with knowledge who are not afraid of working and not afraid of farming in order for industry and agriculture to develop. Modern industry and agriculture are not simple matters. Modern industry and agriculture are technical work. If people with knowledge are afraid of labor and do not move, industry and agriculture will certainly not be easy to progress. We often see students who graduate from engineering and agricultural colleges or vocational schools at home and abroad, because they are afraid of labor, so they only know some theories of industry and agriculture, and cannot be competent to take on practical careers. This phenomenon is extremely pessimistic. Therefore, modern young people must correct this shortcoming of scholars in the past. Modern young people must have a spirit of enjoying labor in order to be good citizens and save China.

Fourth, young people should have a spirit of public service and justice. Callousness is a major flaw in our national character, as mentioned above. Seeing someone injured by a car on the road, and everyone watching without knowing how to help, is a manifestation of callousness. When there are floods or droughts in area A, people in area B, or even wealthy people in area A, indulge in pleasure and do not know how to contribute, which is also a manifestation of callousness. When the country is destroyed, those who are prepared to be slaves to the invaders, and even shamelessly serve the enemy and become ministers of a false country, are also manifestations of callousness. If this kind of inferiority is not eliminated, the nation will not have hope. But how to eliminate this callousness? Only by promoting the spirit of public service and justice. The Boy Scouts' promotion of this spirit is very powerful. I believe that modern young people, whether they join the Boy Scouts or not, should cultivate a spirit of public service and justice, and even more so practice it themselves. When people encounter disasters, they must help. When bystanders are bullied, they must stand up for justice. Be a person with some backbone, don't be too clever, don't just care about one's own interests, and don't talk about loyalty.

We must also know that the spirit of public service and justice is related to the spirit of cooperation and the spirit of martial arts. If one is not eager for public service or justice, the difficulty of cooperation will increase; and the spirit of martial arts will not be easy to cultivate.

Fifth, young people should learn various professions. In the past, Chinese scholars, in the negative sense, were unwilling to be soldiers or work; in the positive sense, they were too fond of being officials. Whether it is the poison of the imperial examination system or not, in today's world, it is necessary to correct this. Being an official is not a bad thing in itself, and administration can also be said to be a profession. But not wanting to have a specialized profession, and only wanting to muddle through in the officialdom, is a very bad thing. If everyone wants to be an official, then first, there must be too many officials, and people are doing more than they should, and politics will not be done well. Second, excellent people will go to the officialdom, and other professions will be affected. The first phenomenon is the modern phenomenon of China, and there is no need to explain it further. The second phenomenon can be explained by the situation in the United States. Americans like to make money as much as Chinese like to be officials. If the Chinese are obsessed with being officials, the Americans can be said to be obsessed with money. In the United States, doing business and being a lawyer are very lucrative, while being an official is very unprofitable, even less than being a university professor. Therefore, there are no outstanding talents in the American political world. China is the opposite. There are indeed many talented people in the Chinese political world. However, there cannot be too many people in the political world, because there are too many people in the Chinese political world, and other sectors feel a lack of talent, and politics is chaotic because there are too many people. If young people can, from today onwards, according to their interests, learn a profession, then in various professions, the law of supply and demand can be implemented, and there will be no lack of talent, and there will be no problem of too many people in the political world.

Sixth, young people should prepare to participate in politics. Learning a profession does not mean that you do not need to care about politics. Politics is something that everyone should care about. The meaning of learning a profession is only to restrict those who want to be officials. Caring about politics is different from being an official. There cannot be one more person who wants to be an official, but there cannot be one person who does not care about politics. The problem in China in the past was that scholars wanted to be officials, and illiterate people did not care about politics. As a result, there were too many officials, but too few people cared about politics. To eliminate this abuse, on the one hand, we must hope that everyone has a specialized profession, so that there will not be too many officials. On the other hand, no matter what profession you are in, you must be interested in politics and you must care about politics. The ancients said, "Everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." This means that everyone has a responsibility for the affairs of the country. This also means that everyone must care about the country's politics.

Then how can you be qualified to care about politics? First, you must pay attention to national affairs, including domestic affairs and international affairs; second, you must receive training in the four political powers.

You must pay attention to national affairs. Today's youth, on the one hand, still have too many people who want to be officials, and on the other hand, not enough people pay attention to national affairs. Judging from the matter of students reading newspapers, I can paraphrase a saying of Confucius: "I have not seen anyone who likes to read political news as much as they like to read sports news or social news." This is not a good phenomenon. To care about politics, you must be familiar with the situation of politics. The general understanding of Chinese middle school students of their own country's politics is far less than the general understanding of British and American middle school students of British and American politics. This is why the ability and interest of our Chinese people to care about politics is far behind the ability and interest of British and American people to care about politics.

However, knowing only the political situation and not knowing how to use the four powers is also useless. The so-called four powers are initiation, referendum, election, and recall. Initiation is the power of the people to propose legislation and request the legislative body to pass it. Referendum is the power of the people to vote for or against legislation that has been passed by the legislative body. Election is the power to elect public officials. Recall is the extreme of the people voting on whether to remove public officials from their posts: According to the Premier's Five-Power Constitution, these four political powers are exercised by the people, or exercised by the National Assembly on behalf of the people by voting. No matter how you explain it, to have the ability to care about politics, you must first have the ability to use these four political powers. Therefore, the training to use these four powers is something that young people must not neglect.

The six points listed above are all indispensable conditions for good Chinese citizens. If young people can take the lead and strive to possess the above six conditions, then in ten or twenty years, the knowledge and ability of the Chinese people will be greatly improved, and the work of saving the country will not be difficult to lead. Of course, in addition to these six points, there are other points that young citizens should pay attention to, but the above six are the most important.

Today's ambitious and outstanding young people, many of them hold pessimistic attitudes towards the country. I also acknowledge the dangers of the country and the chaos of society, but pessimism is not a solution. I advise you young people to work hard to understand our country, and work hard to be good citizens. The more you work hard, the less time you have to be pessimistic. The more good citizens there are, the more hope the country has. Young people, you must fulfill your responsibilities to be worthy of the country.

Local News

City Party Headquarters Passed Yesterday: Commemoration Methods for Premier's Birthday

All city agencies, etc., will fly flags and have holidays

According to Guomin News Agency, this month's 12th is the anniversary of the Premier's birth. For the sake of celebration, the city's Party Headquarters has formulated commemoration methods in accordance with the central government's regulations, which were approved at yesterday's regular meeting, and Committee Member Huang Zaoxiong was appointed as the chairman of the conference. At 9:00 AM that day, representatives from all walks of life will be convened at the Public Education Hall on Wenmiao Road to hold a commemoration meeting. All city agencies, groups, schools, and party headquarters at all levels will have a day off and fly flags to celebrate. The commemoration methods are recorded as follows: (1) Convene the Shanghai Municipal People's Premier's Birthday Commemoration Representative Conference; (2) The venue is the Public Education Hall on Wenmiao Road; (3) The date is November 12th at 9:00 AM; (4) The chairman of the conference will be served by a member of the municipal executive committee; (5) Publish a notice in the newspaper for three days starting on November 10th, 1. All sectors of society will have a day off on this day and fly flags to celebrate, in order to extend the commemoration; 2. All municipal organizations, groups, and party headquarters at all levels must participate; (6) Send a letter to the municipal education bureau to instruct all schools in the city to send ten representatives with a letter to participate; (7) Send a letter to the municipal public security bureau to instruct the police to maintain order at the venue and send a military band to participate; (8) The matters of hospitality, arrangement, and master of ceremonies of the conference will be handled by the propaganda section, and the matters of discipline will be handled by the investigation section; (9) The text for the Premier's Birthday Commemoration will be drafted by the propaganda section.

After the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Committee Closed, Li, Huang, and Others Returned to Shanghai Yesterday

Central Committee members Li Shizeng, Huang Jilu, Li Renren, Deng Qingyang, Zhan Jusi, and Cui Guangxi, et al., went to Beijing a few days ago to attend the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Committee. Now that the plenary session has ended, they took the night train together from Beijing to Shanghai on the evening of the 11th. They arrived at the North Station at 7:15 yesterday morning and got off the train. Li immediately returned to his private residence on Fucaissen Road. Fujian Chairman Chen Yi Flew to Shanghai Yesterday

Scheduled to Go to Beijing Today

Chen Yi, Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, accompanied by Li Jiaju, Chief of Staff of the Fujian Provincial Pacification Office, flew from Fuzhou to Shanghai on a China Aviation Corporation Luoling aircraft at 11:25 yesterday morning. He arrived in Shanghai at about 3:00 in the afternoon. After getting off the plane, Chen returned to the Qi residence in Zhangjia Garden on Jing'an Temple Road to rest. Then, at about 4:00, he met with a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency to talk about the recent situation in Fujian Province. Chen is scheduled to take the night express train to Beijing tonight. The details are recorded as follows.

Welcoming Personnel: When Chen arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon, those who went to welcome him in the local area included Li Zeyi, advisor to Fujian Province, Wang Changchun, commissioner of the municipal government, Wang Dasui, inspector general of the municipal public security bureau, Gan Hailan, adjutant of the garrison headquarters, Japanese Lieutenant General Banshi, and many relatives and friends. After Chen got off the plane and exchanged greetings with the welcoming personnel, he immediately changed to a car and went directly to the Qi residence to rest.

Fujian Province's Finances: A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency interviewed Chen at his Qi residence. According to the conversation, the province's finances are quite difficult, with a monthly shortage of about 10 million yuan. However, education, military affairs, etc., are not reduced due to the economic impact, and progress is still being made step by step. As for the legal tender issued by the Ministry of Finance this time, the market in Fujian Province has not been affected much, and prices have not increased. This is because there are fewer speculators spreading rumors in Fujian Province, which is not comparable to Shanghai. The Fuzhou Bank has branches of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Southeast World Bank, etc., which will of course handle matters in accordance with the orders of the Ministry of Finance without any problems.

Mission to Taiwan: The situation in Fujian Province is extremely peaceful. The remnant bandits in the Fujian-Zhejiang border area will soon be eliminated. Because there were disturbances in Taiwan from time to time, I went to Taiwan at the end of last month to visit the expo, and conveniently had some contact with the authorities in Taiwan. Therefore, the public security in Fujian Province will become more stable in the future.

Going to Beijing Tonight: It is also learned that Chen is scheduled to take the night express train to Beijing at 11:00 tonight to attend the Fifth National Congress, visit the authorities, report on the political situation in Fujian Province, and is expected to stay in Beijing for two weeks before returning to Fujian to take charge of affairs.
